# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-103">"呼叫质量" 仪表板中可用的尺寸和测量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-104">Microsoft 团队和 Skype for business Online 的通话质量仪表板（CQD）使你能够更好地了解通过这些服务进行通话的通话质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-105">本主题提供有关通过 CQD 可见的维度和度量的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-106">若要了解有关 CQD 的详细信息，请参阅[打开和使用 Microsoft 团队和 Skype for Business Online 的通话质量仪表板](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-107">第一和第二终结点分类</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-108">CQD 中的许多维度和度量值标记为第一或第二。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-109">以下逻辑用于确定将流或通话中涉及的哪些终结点标为第一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-110">当服务器参与流或呼叫时，首先考虑服务器终结点（AV MCU、中介服务器等）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-111">客户端终结点被视为第二个终结点，除非该流位于两个服务器终结点之间。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-112">如果两个终结点的类型相同，则 "第一个" 与 "第二" 是基于用户代理类别的内部排序设置的，以确保排序一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-113">例如，下面的每一行表示一个流中涉及的一对用户代理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-114">呼叫方的用户代理类别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-114">User Agent Category of Caller</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-115">被叫方的用户代理类别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-115">User Agent Category of Callee</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-116">First Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-116">First Endpoint</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-117">Second Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-117">Second Endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-118">First Is Caller</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-118">First Is Caller</span></span>
|:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-119">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-119">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-120">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-120">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-121">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-121">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-122">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-122">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-123">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-123">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-124">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-124">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-125">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-125">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-126">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-126">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-127">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-127">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-128">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-128">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-129">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-129">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-130">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-130">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-131">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-131">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-132">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-132">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-133">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-133">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-134">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-134">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-135">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-135">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-136">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-136">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-137">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-137">AV-MCU</span></span> ||
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-138">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-138">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-139">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-139">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-140">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-140">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-141">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-141">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-142">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-142">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-143">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-143">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-144">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-144">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-145">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-145">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-146">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-146">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-147">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-147">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-148">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-148">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-149">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-149">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-150">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-150">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-151">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-151">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-152">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-152">FALSE</span></span> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-p103">[!注释] 第一和第二分类与终结点是呼叫方还是被叫方无关。"第一是呼叫方"维度可以用来帮助确定哪个终结点是呼叫方或被叫方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-p103">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee. The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-155">维度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-156">维度信息基于上载到 CQD 门户的数据的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-157">许多维度值也可以用作筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-158">下表按查询编辑器中列出的顺序列出了 CQD 中当前可用的维度，这些维度是用于创建报表或编辑以前定义的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-159">名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-159">Name</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-160">数据类型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-160">Data type</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-161">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-161">Description</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-162">空值的可能原因</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-162">Possible Reasons for blank values</span></span> |

| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-164">First CPU Name</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-164">First CPU Name</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-165">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-165">String</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-166">第一终结点使用的 CPU 的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-166">Name of the CPU used by the first endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-167">**示例值：** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-167">**Example value:** Contoso CPU X11 @ 1.80 GHz</span></span> | <br/><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-168">&bull;终结点未报告此数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-168">&bull; This data was not reported by the endpoint</span></span>   |

class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2385">:</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2386">: 直接</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2386">: DIRECT</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2387">: 失败</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2387">: FAILED</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2388">: HTTP</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2388">: HTTP</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2389">: 中继</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2389">: RELAY</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2390">表示每个终结点使用的 ICE 连接类型的成对值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2390">Pair of type of ICE connectivity used by each endpoint.</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2391">&bull;终结点使用的 ICE 连接未知或未报告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2391">&bull; ICE connectivity used by endpoint was not known or reported</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2392">OS Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2392">OS Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2393">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2393">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2394">表示第一和第二终结点的操作系统名称和版本的成对值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2394">Pair of the OS name and version for first and second endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2395">**示例值：** Windows 10： Windows 10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2395">**Example value:** Windows 10 : Windows 10</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2396">&bull;无法解析操作系统名称或终结点未报告操作系统名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2396">&bull; OS name could not be parsed or was not reported by endpoint</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2397">Tenant Id Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2397">Tenant Id Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2398">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2398">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2399">表示第一和第二终结点的租户 ID 的成对值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2399">Pair of the tenant ids for first and second endpoint.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2400">**示例值：** 00000000 （0000-0000-0000-000000000000: 00000000-0000-0000-0000）000000000000</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2400">**Example value:** 00000000 — 0000 - 0000 - 0000 — 000000000000 : 00000000 — 0000 - 0000 - 0000 — 000000000000</span></span>  |  <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2401">&bull;无法确定租户标识符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2401">&bull; The tenant identifier could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2402">当终结点登录到了本地 Skype for Business Server 部署时可能会出现此情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2402">This may happen if endpoint is signed in to an on-premise Skype for Business Server deployment.</span></span>  |
| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2403">Building Name Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2403">Building Name Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2404">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2404">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2405">表示第一和第二终结点的建筑物名称的成对值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2405">Pair of the building name for the first and second endpoint.</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2406">&bull;无法确定终结点的建筑物名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2406">&bull; The building name for an endpoint could not be determined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2407">这可能是因为终结点位于企业网络外部，或正在从没有子网映射的站点访问网络。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2407">This could be because the endpoint is located outside the corporate network, or is accessing the network from a site without a subnet mapping.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2408">**示例值：** 主建筑物：分支网站构建</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2408">**Example value:** Main Building : Branch Site Building</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2409">Inside Corp Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2409">Inside Corp Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2410">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2410">Enumerated pair</span></span> <br/><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2411">**可能的值：**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2411">**Possible values:**</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2412">内部 : 内部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2412">Inside : Inside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2413">内部 : 外部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2413">Inside : Outside</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2414">外部 : 外部</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2414">Outside : Outside</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2415">根据子网映射，显示终结点位于企业网络内部还是外部的成对值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2415">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping.</span></span>   |   |
| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2416">Scenario Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2416">Scenario Pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2417">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2417">Enumerated pair</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2418">显示终结点位于企业网络内部还是外部（根据子网映射确定）以及网络连接详情的成对值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2418">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping and the network connection detail.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2419">**注意：** 对用 "--" 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2419">**Note:** The pairs are separated by '--'.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2420">**示例值：** 客户端内部-客户端内部-wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2420">**Example value:** Client-Inside--Client-Inside-wifi</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2421">&bull;两个终结点或这两个终结点的网络连接类型均未知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2421">&bull; The network connectivity type was unknown for either or both endpoints.</span></span>  |
||||

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2422">有关维度数据类型/单位的注释</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2422">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2423">Boolean</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2423">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2424">布尔值始终为 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2424">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2425">在某些情况下，True 还可以表示为1，False 可以表示为0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2425">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2426">范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2426">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2427">按范围或分组表示的维度值使用以下格式显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2427">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2428">_\<排序顺序字符串\> [\<下限非\> - \<独占上限\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2428">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2429">例如，持续时间（分钟）维度表示以分钟为单位的通话持续时间，报告的值以取值范围的形式表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2429">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2430">Duration (Minutes)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2430">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2431">解释方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2431">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2432">062: [0 - 0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2432">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2433">流持续时间 = 0 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2433">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2434">064: [1 - 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2434">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2435">1 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 2 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2435">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2436">065: [2 - 3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2436">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2437">2 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 3 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2437">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2438">066： [3 –4）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2438">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2439">3 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 4 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2439">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2440">\<排序顺序字符串> 用于在呈现数据时控制排序顺序，并且可用于筛选。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2440">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2441">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2441">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2442">[!注释] 排序字符串的实际值并不重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2442">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2443">枚举字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2443">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2444">CQD 使用的字符串通常派生自数据文件，它们几乎可以是允许长度内的任何字符组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2444">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2445">某些维度看起来像是字符串，但由于它们只能是预定义值的简短列表之一，因此它们是枚举而不是真正的字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2445">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2446">某些枚举字符串也会成对使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2446">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2447">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2447">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2448">按枚举对表示的维度使用以下格式显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2448">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2449">_\<一个终结点的枚举值\> ： \<来自其他终结点的枚举值\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2449">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2450">枚举值的顺序一致，但此顺序不反映第一或第二终结点的顺序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2450">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2451">例如，网络连接详情对显示两个终结点的网络连接详情值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2451">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2452">Network Connection Detail Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2452">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2453">解释方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2453">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2454">有线 : 有线</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2454">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2455">第一和第二终结点均使用有线以太网连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2455">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2456">有线 : wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2456">Wired : wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2457">第一个终结点使用有线以太网连接且第二个终结点使用 Wi-Fi 连接，或第二个终结点使用有线以太网连接且第一个终结点使用 Wi-Fi 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2457">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2458">: wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2458">: wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2459">第一个终结点使用 WiFi 连接且第二个终结点使用的网络连接未知，或第二个终结点使用 WiFi 连接且第一个终结点使用的网络连接未知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2459">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span> |
| | |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2460">空值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2460">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2461">上表列出了维度可能出现空值的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2461">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2462">如果 QoE 记录的可用维度为 false，则许多维度和度量值将为空。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2462">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2463">这通常出现在通话未能成功建立的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2463">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

## <a name="measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2464">计量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2464">Measurements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2465">许多度量值也可以用作筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2465">Many Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2466">下表列出了 CQD 中当前可用的度量值，按查询编辑器中列出的顺序显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2466">The following table lists the measurements currently available in CQD, shown in the order listed in the Query Editor:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2467">衡量指标名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2467">Measure Name</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2468">单位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2468">Units</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2469">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2469">Description</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2470">Total Stream Count</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2470">Total Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2471">流的数量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2471">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2472">媒体流的数量，不区分媒体的类型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2472">Number media streams regardless of type of media.</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2473">CDR 可用流计数总数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2473">Total CDR Available Stream Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2474">流的数量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2474">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2475">可用可靠性/诊断信息的媒体流的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2475">Number of media streams with reliability/diagnostics information available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2476">请参阅[Skype For Business 服务器中的呼叫详细记录（CDR）](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/manage/health-and-monitoring/call-detail-recording-cdr)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2476">See [Call detail recording (CDR) in Skype for Business Server](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/manage/health-and-monitoring/call-detail-recording-cdr)</span></span> |

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2993">筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2993">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2994">许多维度和度量值也可以用作筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2994">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4f95f-2995">你可以在查询中使用筛选器来消除信息，方法与选择维度或度量以在查询中添加或包含信息的方式相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4f95f-2995">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
